  386\t   * Convert report to Discord embed format\n   387\t   * @param {object}
report - Report object\n   388\t   * @returns {object} Discord embed object\n   
389\t   */\n   390\t  toDiscordEmbed(report) {\n   391\t    const colors = {\n  
392\t      \'daily-summary\': 0x3498db,    // Blue\n   393\t      \'stock\': 0x2
ecc71,           // Green\n   394\t      \'error\': 0xe74c3c,           // Red\n
  395\t      \'memory-cleanup\': 0x9b59b6,  // Purple\n   396\t      \'token\': 
0xf1c40f,           // Yellow\n   397\t      \'backup\': 0x1abc9c,          // T
eal\n   398\t      \'issue\': 0xe67e22,           // Orange\n   399\t      \'hea
lth\': 0x34495e,          // Dark\n   400\t      \'reminder\': 0x95a5a6,        
// Gray\n   401\t      \'system-check\': 0x9b59b6     // Purple for system check
\n   402\t    };\n   403\t\n   404\t    // Truncate content if too long (Discord
field value limit is 1024 chars)\n   405\t    const truncate = (text, maxLen = 1
024) => {\n   406\t      if (!text) return \'(No data)\';\n   407\t      if (tex
t.length <= maxLen) return text;\n   408\t      return text.substring(0, maxLen 
- 3) + \'...\';\n   409\t    };\n   410\t\n   411\t    // Determine inline based
on section name (not inline for longer content)\n   412\t    const shouldInline 
= (sectionName) => {\n   413\t      const noInlineSections = [\'提醒事項\', \'活
躍錯誤\', \'腳本\'];\n   414\t      return !noInlineSections.some(s => sectionNa
me.includes(s));\n   415\t    };\n   416\t\n   417\t    const embed = {\n   418\
t      title: report.title,\n   419\t      color: colors[report.metadata?.templa
teName] || 0x3498db,\n   420\t      fields: report.sections.map(section => ({\n 
 421\t        name: truncate(section.name, 256),  // Discord limit for name is 2
56\n   422\t        value: truncate(section.content || \'(No data)\'),\n   423\t
       inline: shouldInline(section.name)\n   424\t      })),\n   425\t      foo
ter: {\n   426\t        text: `Generated: ${report.generatedAt}`\n   427\t      
},\n   428\t      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n   429\t    };\n   430\t\
n   431\t    // Add metadata as description if available\n   432\t    if (report
.metadata) {\n   433\t      const metaText = Object.entries(report.metadata)\n  
434\t        .map(([key, value]) => `${key}: ${value}`)\n   435\t        .join(\
' | \');\n   436\t      embed.description = truncate(metaText, 4096);  // Discor
d description limit\n   437\t    }\n   438\t\n   439\t    return embed;\n   440\
t  }\n   441\t\n   442\t  /**\n   443\t   * Convert data array to markdown table
format\n   444\t   * @param {Array<object>} data - Array of data objects\n   445
\t   * @param {Array<object>} columns - Column definitions [{key, header, align}
]\n   446\t   * @returns {string} Markdown formatted table\n   447\t   */\n   44
8\t  toTable(data, columns) {\n   449\t    if (!Array.isArray(data) || data.leng
th === 0) {\n   450\t      return \'(No data)\';\n   451\t    }\n   452\t\n   45
3\t    if (!Array.isArray(columns) || columns.length === 0) {\n   454\t      thr
ow new Error(\'Columns definition is required\');\n   455\t    }\n   456\t\n   4
57\t    // Validate column definitions\n   458\t    columns.forEach((col, idx) =
> {\n   459\t      if (!col.key || !col.header) {\n   460\t        throw new Err
or(`Column ${idx} must have \'key\' and \'header\' properties`);\n   461\t      
}\n   462\t    });\n   463\t\n   464\t    // Build header row\n   465\t    const
header = columns.map(c => c.header).join(\' | \');\n   466\t\n   467\t    // Bui
ld separator row with alignment\n   468\t    const separator = columns.map(c => 
{\n   469\t      const align = c.align || \'left\';\n   470\t      if (align ===
\'center\') return \':---:\';\n   471\t      if (align === \'right\') return \'-
--:\';\n   472\t      return \'---\';  // left align (default)\n   473\t    }).j
oin(\' | \');\n   474\t\n   475\t    // Build data rows\n   476\t    const rows 
= data.map(item =>\n   477\t      columns.map(c => {\n   478\t        const valu
e = item[c.key];\n   479\t        // Handle null/undefined\n   480\t        if (
value === null || value === undefined) return \'\';\n   481\t        // Convert 
to string and escape pipe characters\n   482\t        return String(value).repla
ce(/\\|/g, \'\\\\|\');\n   483\t      }).join(\' | \')\n   484\t    );\n   485\t
\n   486\t    return [header, separator, ...rows].join(\'\\n\');\n   487\t  }\n 
 488\t}\n   489\t\n   490\t// ==================================================
